  <script>
   wbq.push(function manageHamburgerMenu() {
  var $nav = $('.js__nav');
  var $navCloseBtn = $('#nav-close-btn');
  var $navToggleBtn = $('.js__btn--nav-toggle');

  function lockNavFocus() {
    $navCloseBtn.focus();
    document.addEventListener('focusin', focusNavCloseBtn);
  }

  function focusNavCloseBtn(event) {
    if (!$.contains(document.getElementById('masthead-nav'), event.target)) {
      $navCloseBtn.focus();
    }
  }

  function unlockNavFocus() {
    document.removeEventListener('focusin', focusNavCloseBtn);
    $navToggleBtn.focus();
  }

  // hamburger menu to toggle mobile nav, full screen hit area beneath
  // mobile nav to act as toggle target
  $navToggleBtn.click(function (event) {
    $nav.toggleClass('nav--is-open');
    if ($nav.hasClass('nav--is-open')) {
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        lockNavFocus();
      }
      window.TMZ.utils.setAccessibilityFocusTrap('masthead-nav');
      $nav.css('visibility', 'visible');
    } else {
      window.TMZ.utils.removeAccessibilityFocusTrap();
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        unlockNavFocus();
        $navToggleBtn.focus();
      }
      setTimeout(function () {
        $nav.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    }

    event.preventDefault();
  });
});
  </script>
  <!--/.nav-->

  <script>
   wbq.push(function manageTipMenu() {
  var $tip = $('.js__tip');
  var $tipCloseBtn = $('#tip__btn-close');
  var $tipToggleBtn = $('.js__btn--tip-toggle');
  var $nav = $('.js__nav');

  function lockTipFocus() {
    $tipCloseBtn.focus();
    document.addEventListener('focusin', focusTipCloseBtn);
  }

  function focusTipCloseBtn(event) {
    if (!$.contains(document.getElementById('tip'), event.target)) {
      $tipCloseBtn.focus();
    }
  }

  function unlockTipFocus() {
    document.removeEventListener('focusin', focusTipCloseBtn);
  }

  // toggle tip full screen mobile menu
  $tipToggleBtn.click(function (event) {
    $tip.toggleClass('tip--is-open');
    if ($tip.hasClass('tip--is-open')) {
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        lockTipFocus();
      }
      window.TMZ.utils.setAccessibilityFocusTrap('tip');
      $tip.css('visibility', 'visible');
      setTimeout(function() {
        $nav.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    } else {
      window.TMZ.utils.removeAccessibilityFocusTrap();
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        unlockTipFocus();
        $tipToggleBtn.focus();
      }
      setTimeout(function() {
        $tip.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    }

    // Hide nav
    if ($nav.hasClass('nav--is-open')) {
      setTimeout(function () {
        $nav.removeClass('nav--is-open');
      }, 300);
    }
    event.preventDefault();
  });
});
  </script>

         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/donald-trump/">
           <strong>
            Donald Trump
           </strong>
          </a>
          had to know his first trip back to NYC since leaving the White House would be a turbulent one ... and the Big Apple is delivering.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-9698e5c6e0806f086633b0a959d36c79-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-25a9ee00953a9edceaa9827b392e3da3">
         <p>
          There are about a dozen or so protesters outside Trump Tower in Manhattan waving a huge "Arrest Trump" banner. There's also a giant inflatable caricature of Trump and others are holding signs that read "Go Home Florida Man" and "Indict Trump."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-25a9ee00953a9edceaa9827b392e3da3-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-f9a263642eaaee5855d81a1335f86d15">

         <p>
          It ain't all bad news for 45 in the Democratic stronghold of NYC -- a throng of Trump supporters also gathered nearby pumping up his potential return to the
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/02/28/donald-trump-teases-2024-white-house-run-cpac-speech/">
           <strong>
            Oval Office in 2024
           </strong>
          </a>
          .
         </p>

        <!--/#cb-e9dd3e8fdc242c544b705d02e75b98b2-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-3d6a126d40ceb9d92ca83ddd87057785">
         <p>
          It's unclear what brought Trump, who arrived Sunday night, back to his old stomping grounds ... but it could be tied to his legal problems. The Manhattan D.A.'s Office is currently investigating Trump for tax and bank-related fraud.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-3d6a126d40ceb9d92ca83ddd87057785-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-837340e76a2627897ffdd2b3377ea18c">
         <p>
          Remember ... Trump's been living at Mar-a-Lago since leaving office, and he officially changed his address from NY to FLA back in 2019. Seems wherever Trump goes ...
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/01/24/trump-greeted-skywriter-banner-plane-mar-a-lago-pathetic-loser/">
           <strong>
            so do banners
           </strong>
          </a>
          .

         <h2 class="article__header-title">

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first" id="cb-216b2d757e977ee523e47902adf4d139">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/9e/4by3/2021/03/08/9ef9269c94bc42cd9b5e34253afde793_md.jpg"/>

           </span>
          </div>

        <!--/#cb-216b2d757e977ee523e47902adf4d139-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-666a8393488013a4d293b5a1ffc55160">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/meghan-markle/">
           <strong>
            Meghan Markle
           </strong>
          </a>
          and
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/prince-harry/">
           <strong>
            Prince Harry
           </strong>
          </a>
          may think they officially tied the knot in a secret wedding 3 days before their televised one -- but we've learned the church doesn't see it that way.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-666a8393488013a4d293b5a1ffc55160-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-3b43b8b359fbb15bda4629f6478d0b9e">
         <p>
          A source within the church tells TMZ ... a marriage must be solemnized by a member of the clergy in a church or in a place specified in a special license -- be it a cathedral, chapel or hospital -- AND in the presence of 2 witnesses.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-3b43b8b359fbb15bda4629f6478d0b9e-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-a569559f7791c7d23ce21b9cbba0ec7a">
         <p>
          That last part is key, because Meghan told
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/oprah-winfrey/">
           <strong>
            Oprah
           </strong>
          </a>
          she and Harry got married prior to the big royal wedding we all saw -- in their backyard with only the Archbishop of Canterbury
          <strong>
           Justin Welby
          </strong>
          . So, they'd be one witness short of a real marriage.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-a569559f7791c7d23ce21b9cbba0ec7a-->

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-2b119f27-1809-4ba4-8013-1b0b93a699df-1668238645-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-2b119f27-1809-4ba4-8013-1b0b93a699df-1668238645-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-2b119f27-1809-4ba4-8013-1b0b93a699df-1668238645-footer');
            hideSpinner();
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-2b119f27-1809-4ba4-8013-1b0b93a699df-1668238645-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-2b119f27-1809-4ba4-8013-1b0b93a699df-1668238645-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-2b119f27-1809-4ba4-8013-1b0b93a699df-1668238645-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-2b119f27-1809-4ba4-8013-1b0b93a699df-1668238645-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-2b119f27-1809-4ba4-8013-1b0b93a699df-1668238645'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-2b119f27-1809-4ba4-8013-1b0b93a699df-1668238645-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-2b119f27-1809-4ba4-8013-1b0b93a699df-1668238645-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-08-030821-meghan-harry-marriage-1051930/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:2b119f27-1809-4ba4-8013-1b0b93a699df',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });

          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/07/meghan-markle-accuses-royal-family-racism-archie-dark-skin/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" title="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/07/meghan-markle-accuses-royal-family-racism-archie-dark-skin/">

      <article class="article" id="blogroll-d5a75f41-ee36-4154-9987-0043271be662">
       <div class="article__channel--reporting">
       </div>
       <header class="article__header">
        <a class="article__header-link js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"headline","pos":3}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:d5a75f41-ee36-4154-9987-0043271be662" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/08/papa-johns-founder-john-schnatter-rid-of-n-word-vocabulary-racism-ousting/">
         <h2 class="article__header-title">
          <span class="article__hf1 text-uppercase h3">
           Papa John's Founder
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf2 text-none h2">
           I Tried Scrubbing N-Word from My History
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf3 text-uppercase h1">
           FOR 20 MONTHS!!!
          </span>
         </h2>
        </a>
        <h5 class="article__published-at">
         <ul class="social social--sm">
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Facebook" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--facebook js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"facebook-header","pos":3}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:d5a75f41-ee36-4154-9987-0043271be662" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/08/papa-johns-founder-john-schnatter-rid-of-n-word-vocabulary-racism-ousting/" onclick="window.open('http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F08%2Fpapa-johns-founder-john-schnatter-rid-of-n-word-vocabulary-racism-ousting%2F', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">
            <span aria-label="Facebook" class="icon icon-facebook--white social__icon--facebook" role="img">
            </span>
            <span class="social__count">
             1.5K
            </span>
            <span class="sr-only">
             shares
            </span>
           </a>
          </li>
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Twitter" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--twitter js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"twitter-header","pos":3}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:d5a75f41-ee36-4154-9987-0043271be662" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/08/papa-johns-founder-john-schnatter-rid-of-n-word-vocabulary-racism-ousting/" onclick="window.open('https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F08%2Fpapa-johns-founder-john-schnatter-rid-of-n-word-vocabulary-racism-ousting%2F&amp;text=Papa%20John%27s%20Founder%20Doesn%27t%20Want%20N-Word%20Tied%20to%20Him%2C%20Trying%20to%20Convince%20Media&amp;via=TMZ&amp;related=HarveyLevinTMZ', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">
            <span aria-label="Twitter" class="icon icon-sd icon-twitter--white" role="img">
            </span>
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <!--/.social-->
         3/8/2021 12:27 PM PT
        </h5>
        <!--/.article__posted-date-->
       </header>
       <div class="article__blocks">
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first" id="cb-24be5f1380f5518ff23f1cf213db7237">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/97/4by3/2021/03/08/975e7d19c98e47248a305039252284eb_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Getty
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-24be5f1380f5518ff23f1cf213db7237-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default updated" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-8eeda1ec8975b8735dd733a7fcda86bf">
         <p>
          <strong class="updated-time--strong">
           3:03 PM PT
          </strong>
          -- John wants to make one thing clear, telling us it didn't take him 20 months to stop using the n-word, but instead, he's spent that long trying to get the media to stop tying to him.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-8eeda1ec8975b8735dd733a7fcda86bf-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default updated" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-ce03bdd3282ca9f1bcec3e56c265e9b7">
         <p>
          John says during his OAN interview, what he meant to say was, "Get rid of this n-word in (the) vocabulary and dictionary (of the news media), and everything else because it’s just not true," – reflecting my commitment to correct the false and malicious reporting by the news media about the conference call."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-ce03bdd3282ca9f1bcec3e56c265e9b7-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default updated" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-5c1ef316ccf201772b4ec4c993ad8f0d">
         <p>
          John maintains that the audio of him using the n-word in the audio released in 2018 was taken out of context, and that he immediately followed it up with "I never used the word" ... though he says that aspect of the call was largely overlooked.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-5c1ef316ccf201772b4ec4c993ad8f0d-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-cdb404e42f5a9fa08575875c19848d6f">
         <p>
          Ousted Papa John's founder,
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/john-schnatter/">
           <strong>
            John Schnatter
           </strong>
          </a>
          , is talking in doublespeak ... insisting he's not racist, but copping to having to purge the n-word from his repertoire to prove it.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-cdb404e42f5a9fa08575875c19848d6f-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-2cb23e14c00dcbb551ca1d4d3e2daba5">
         <p>
          The former CEO of the pizza chain -- who got the boot a few years back for allegedly uttering the n-word in a conference call -- made an appearance on the far-right news channel, OAN ... where he was rehashing his experience, which he paints as a de facto coup.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-2cb23e14c00dcbb551ca1d4d3e2daba5-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-07eab41c3ca875f524fc95f19a02dfa8">
         <p>
          At one point, Schnatter says the Board wrongly
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2018/07/11/papa-johns-john-schnatter-n-word-resigns-university-of-louisville-trustees/">
           <strong>
            portrayed him as a racist
           </strong>
          </a>
          -- adding he's been up at night since then, wondering how they got away with it.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-07eab41c3ca875f524fc95f19a02dfa8-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-twitter-tweet-block canvas-twitter-tweet-block-blogroll canvas-twitter-tweet-block--default" id="cb-041e89bb07c532b10194c203179a8c55">
         <div class="d-flex justify-content-center" id="cb-041e89bb07c532b10194c203179a8c55-5357443-target">
          <blockquote class="twitter-tweet">

            <a href="https://twitter.com/mount_bees?ref_src=twsrc^tfw">
             @mount_bees
            </a>
            )
            <a href="https://t.co/8heITnJJxA">
             pic.twitter.com/8heITnJJxA

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-09b416887f9674c00c47498034a96dfa">
         <p>
          Then comes the contradictory line ... JS says for the past 20 months, he's had 3 goals -- 1) "to get rid of this n-word in my vocabulary and dictionary and everything else because it's just not true," 2) figuring how they did this and 3) to get on with his life.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-09b416887f9674c00c47498034a96dfa-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-549fbdfd3ea44c0c4e40c4f179a2fa04">
         <p>
          That first goal is a doozy to unpack. On its face, it sounds like he's admitting the n-word is a regular thing that shows up in his convos all the time, and that he's needed 20 months to exorcise himself of it.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-549fbdfd3ea44c0c4e40c4f179a2fa04-->

        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.

        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-19d5b25e-f158-5270-960d-bc70cbd10358-964760097-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video

          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-19d5b25e-f158-5270-960d-bc70cbd10358-964760097-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-19d5b25e-f158-5270-960d-bc70cbd10358-964760097-footer');
            hideSpinner();
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-19d5b25e-f158-5270-960d-bc70cbd10358-964760097-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-19d5b25e-f158-5270-960d-bc70cbd10358-964760097-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-19d5b25e-f158-5270-960d-bc70cbd10358-964760097-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-19d5b25e-f158-5270-960d-bc70cbd10358-964760097-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');

              document.getElementById('video-player-19d5b25e-f158-5270-960d-bc70cbd10358-964760097-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-19d5b25e-f158-5270-960d-bc70cbd10358-964760097-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/112619-john-schnatter-4682571-0-qn6nc5g9/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:19d5b25e-f158-5270-960d-bc70cbd10358',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });
         </script>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-544d1d9134d69c78b7e3a4c710957b77-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-da58f39df64883e03c304fc08b6690bd">
         <p>
          Something tells us that's not what he meant -- he might've been trying to say "get rid of this n-word scandal" -- but that's certainly not how it came out. BTW, Schnatter keeps putting his foot in his mouth with these TV interviews, intentionally or not.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-da58f39df64883e03c304fc08b6690bd-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-4ad0d22a9d562580187b1ffbd08cdcf7">
         <p>
          Remember, in 2019 ... he did another TV spot where he admitted he'd eaten
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2019/11/26/papa-john-founder-40-pizzas-30-days-ouster-shaq-interview/">
           <strong>
            40 pizzas in 30 days
           </strong>
          </a>
          (to see how they're holding up without him) -- and it just came off as sad and pathetic.
         </p>
        </section>

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-6fa97fd1ce8df73954c09c70f35c6954">

          </strong>

          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/joe-biden/">

          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/jill-biden/">

           </strong>
          </a>
          had any reaction following Meghan's claims of racism against the Royal Family.

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-741c40d9-dc6f-420c-9db8-1d82a21498fa-1506520842-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-741c40d9-dc6f-420c-9db8-1d82a21498fa-1506520842-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-741c40d9-dc6f-420c-9db8-1d82a21498fa-1506520842-footer');
            hideSpinner();
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-741c40d9-dc6f-420c-9db8-1d82a21498fa-1506520842-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-741c40d9-dc6f-420c-9db8-1d82a21498fa-1506520842-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-741c40d9-dc6f-420c-9db8-1d82a21498fa-1506520842-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-741c40d9-dc6f-420c-9db8-1d82a21498fa-1506520842-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-741c40d9-dc6f-420c-9db8-1d82a21498fa-1506520842'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-741c40d9-dc6f-420c-9db8-1d82a21498fa-1506520842-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-741c40d9-dc6f-420c-9db8-1d82a21498fa-1506520842-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-08-030821-jen-psaki-1051866/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:741c40d9-dc6f-420c-9db8-1d82a21498fa',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-faae0ca37de182e0cd4aaca600b44055">
         <p>
          Psaki sidestepped whether the Bidens actually watched the interview, but added ... "For anyone to come forward and speak about their own struggles with mental health and tell their own personal story — that takes courage, and that's certainly something the President believes, and he's talked about the importance of investing in a lot of these areas that they’re committed to in the future as well."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-faae0ca37de182e0cd4aaca600b44055-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-cdc1be95904007fd94f163f137a08e06">
         <p>
          She was careful, though, not to ruffle any feathers across the pond because Psaki also emphasized America's "strong and abiding relationship" with the United Kingdom.
         </p>
        </section>

         <p>
          As you know, Meghan and Harry
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/07/meghan-markle-accuses-royal-family-racism-archie-dark-skin/">
           <strong>

          about her suicidal thoughts and the Royal family members who expressed concern about

           </strong>
          </a>
          possibly being too dark.

          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-1c4f901a-602a-463e-9d02-462f2c2963b0-251729995-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-1c4f901a-602a-463e-9d02-462f2c2963b0-251729995-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-1c4f901a-602a-463e-9d02-462f2c2963b0-251729995-footer');
            hideSpinner();
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-1c4f901a-602a-463e-9d02-462f2c2963b0-251729995-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-1c4f901a-602a-463e-9d02-462f2c2963b0-251729995-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-1c4f901a-602a-463e-9d02-462f2c2963b0-251729995-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-1c4f901a-602a-463e-9d02-462f2c2963b0-251729995-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-1c4f901a-602a-463e-9d02-462f2c2963b0-251729995'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-1c4f901a-602a-463e-9d02-462f2c2963b0-251729995-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-1c4f901a-602a-463e-9d02-462f2c2963b0-251729995-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-08-030821-dr-shola-mos-shogbamimu-1051875/',

                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }

          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-993705930-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-993705930-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-993705930-footer');
            hideSpinner();
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-993705930-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-993705930-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-993705930-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-993705930-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-993705930'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-993705930-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-993705930-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(

                  'tmz:video:8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }

         <p>

          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/naked-cowboy/">
           <strong>
            Naked Cowboy
           </strong>
          </a>
          , famous for performing in Times Square, got busted way down in Florida for his same old schtick ... and cops say his trusty guitar broke when he resisted arrest.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-13ba0f2f5c71cd28836ba027ce89c928-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-1c7e524a835406ca7acbc7ec03604628">
         <p>
          <strong>
           Robert Burck
          </strong>
          , the nearly naked man behind the Naked Cowboy character, was arrested Saturday on a misdemeanor charge of resisting arrest without violence in Daytona Beach, where police also cited him for aggressive panhandling.
         </p>
        </section>

         <p>
          The Naked Cowboy was in town for Bike Week ... and cops say he was in his familiar getup -- white briefs, guitar and a cowboy hat -- when he was taking pictures with folks on the street in exchange for cash.
         </p>

              'enablejsapi': 1,
              'origin': window.location.origin,
            },
          });
      }

      function cueVideo(e) {
        e.target.cueVideoById('MLKTApGd3gQ', 0);
      }

      function insertSwipe(e) {
        var swipeDiv = document.createElement('div');
        swipeDiv.innerText = "Exclusive";
        swipeDiv.classList.add('media-swipe');
        swipeDiv.classList.add('youtube-video-block__media-swipe');
        e.target.getIframe().parentNode.prepend(swipeDiv);
      }

      function fail() {
        $target.html(document.getElementById('cb-dca82beb0535cab7a953d8b7c02cec89-733340455-failed').innerHTML);
      }

      function styleIframe(e) {
        var iframe = e.target.getIframe();
        iframe.classList.add('embed-responsive');
        if (!iframe.getAttribute('width')) {
          iframe.setAttribute('width', targetWidth);
        }
        if (!iframe.getAttribute('height')) {
          iframe.setAttribute('height', targetWidth / (16 / 9));
        }
      }

              window.TMZ.utils.loadYouTubeJs()
          .then(function initYouTubeBlock() {
            initPlayer(function onReady(e) {
              styleIframe(e);
              cueVideo(e);
                                        });
          }).catch(fail);
          });
         </script>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-dca82beb0535cab7a953d8b7c02cec89-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-5636bd55e209a674596b42a5d68ec7bc">
         <p>
          Police say a huge crowd formed around the Naked Cowboy as he hovered near a business on Main Street, so an officer cited him for panhandling. Cops say he refused to follow orders and when he resisted arrest while up against a patrol car the headstock of his guitar broke.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-5636bd55e209a674596b42a5d68ec7bc-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-eee9d7712379eda41ff69138bd1df6c6">
         <p>
          The Naked Cowboy says it was his 21st trip to Daytona Beach Bike Week -- but it sounds like he's worn out his welcome, at least with law enforcement.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-eee9d7712379eda41ff69138bd1df6c6-->
       </div>

         <h2 class="article__header-title">
          <span class="article__hf1 text-uppercase h3">
           Bam Margera
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf2 text-uppercase h1">
           Hospitalized with Staph Infection ...
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf3 text-none h2">
           From Recent Tattoo
          </span>
         </h2>
        </a>
        <h5 class="article__published-at">
         <ul class="social social--sm">
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Facebook" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--facebook js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"facebook-header","pos":7}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:7f155824-d9d6-410d-8065-0db59de82910" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/08/bam-margera-hospitalized-staph-infection-leg-tattoo-hot-tub/" onclick="window.open('http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F08%2Fbam-margera-hospitalized-staph-infection-leg-tattoo-hot-tub%2F', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first" id="cb-aee07213e041e566a569875035f500b4">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/7a/4by3/2021/03/08/7a2c201c423548229c55bc86c53a256a_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="media-swipe image-block__media-swipe">
           Exclusive Details
          </div>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            TMZ.com
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-aee07213e041e566a569875035f500b4-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-b953a57a859b46869ee2dc267bb06809">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/bam-margera/">
           <strong>
            Bam Margera
           </strong>
          </a>
          is learning hot tubs and fresh ink don't mix -- he needed a hospital stay to treat a staph infection from his latest tattoo.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-b953a57a859b46869ee2dc267bb06809-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-7855588f0dbd48c21910ec66022f3692">
         <p>
          The "Jackass" star was hospitalized over the weekend after experiencing pain in the same leg that's home to his new Farsi tatt. Bam's no stranger to pain -- it's kinda been his job for years -- so ya gotta imagine he was really hurting bad.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-7855588f0dbd48c21910ec66022f3692-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-91044cbe2ad9919683a89b29f03d5bc7">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/23/4by3/2021/03/08/23b3709130244faf89ab7e6566682e43_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-91044cbe2ad9919683a89b29f03d5bc7-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-565c7d239bf562704cff32b426c74376">
         <p>
          Bam says he had a staph infection, and sources close to him tell us the leg was likely infected when he went into a hot tub.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-565c7d239bf562704cff32b426c74376-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-fa364b85fc873810b443021418b438f5">
         <p>
          As anyone with tattoos likely knows, you're supposed to take it easy after getting inked up ... and hot tubs really sound like a bad idea, especially with leg tatts. Tough lesson here for Bam.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-fa364b85fc873810b443021418b438f5-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-775ef35b67abd268b4d9827c01d2db8e">
         <p>
          The good news ... we're told he's already been released from the hospital and should make a full recovery.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-775ef35b67abd268b4d9827c01d2db8e-->

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-330436919-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-330436919-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-330436919-footer');
            hideSpinner();
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-330436919-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-330436919-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-330436919-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-330436919-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-330436919'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-330436919-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-330436919-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-08-030821-meghan-markle-oprah-1051465/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });

         <p>
          They made it clear ... this was
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/07/meghan-markle-accuses-royal-family-racism-archie-dark-skin/">
           <strong>
            not just one conversation
           </strong>
          </a>
          , but several while
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/meghan-markle/">
           <strong>
            Meghan
           </strong>
          </a>
          was pregnant. They also made the stunning claim Archie would not get security since he was not a Prince, despite the death threats Harry and his family were enduring. Indeed, they said all security was pulled once they moved to Canada.
         </p>
        </section>

         </p>

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-a851d56c9207b4b651ff917c7ecd9ece">

          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/prince-charles/">
           <strong>
            Prince Charles
           </strong>
          </a>
          , saying when they moved to Canada, Charles stopped taking Harry's calls. He essentially accused his dad of being heartless ... especially given the fact Charles knew the difficulties Harry faced because he had been through something similar with
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/princess-diana/">
           <strong>
            Diana
           </strong>
          </a>
          .

           </strong>

          . It's interesting, Harry intimated to Oprah William feels trapped but he can't leave given his position.

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-d12824898dab130d384ae5b1af2715fd">
         <p>
          Harry says the entire family survives in a "toxic environment," although he says Charles has made peace with it.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-d12824898dab130d384ae5b1af2715fd-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-twitter-tweet-block canvas-twitter-tweet-block-blogroll canvas-twitter-tweet-block--default" id="cb-7e447db2e0220d7be800c118b8f694cd">

         <h2 class="article__header-title">
          <span class="article__hf1 text-uppercase h3">
           George Floyd Case
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf2 text-titlecase h2">
           Supporters Gather at Court
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf3 text-uppercase h1">
           As Chauvin Jury Selection's Delayed
          </span>
         </h2>
        </a>
        <h5 class="article__published-at">
         <ul class="social social--sm">

         <div class="gallery-block">
          <a class="media-link gallery-block__link js-track-link js-click-gallery" data-container-ref="tmz:article:ed207b53-4b5e-4670-9980-0478b46cdb51" data-context='{"name":"gallery-block","section":"blogroll"}' data-node-ref="tmz:gallery:a57a9a7a-1997-4b68-b7c0-7d3cdb7ad4dd" href="https://www.tmz.com/photos/2021/03/08/protest-derek-chauvin-trial-george-floyd-death-photos/" id="gallery-link-a57a9a7a-1997-4b68-b7c0-7d3cdb7ad4dd">

        <!--/#cb-a25c55bc986033c6e4654619974068ef-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-0170c8752be04c1b1085c310d1fd60f6">
         <p>
          A throng of
          <strong>
           George Floyd
          </strong>
          supporters are gathered outside a Minneapolis courthouse for what's supposed to be jury selection day in ex-cop
          <strong>
           Derek Chauvin
          </strong>
          's murder case.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-0170c8752be04c1b1085c310d1fd60f6-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-39cb912b8a1499f7994aaf225d1a9e60">
         <p>
          The judge in the case on Monday paused jury selection for at least a day and said he wants to hear from the State Court of Appeals as to whether a third-degree murder charge can be added to Chauvin's counts. He had reportedly said he would initially start jury selection with the matter unresolved but has now changed course.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-39cb912b8a1499f7994aaf225d1a9e60-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-3e3b07cf9659b68dbb6ebeb904093742">
         <p>
          According to the Minneapolis Star Tribune ... Chauvin's attorney will ask the State Supreme Court to overturn Friday's ruling from the Court of Appeals which said the judge can reinstate the third-degree murder charge. The judge told prospective jurors to be ready to return to court on Tuesday.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-3e3b07cf9659b68dbb6ebeb904093742-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-ceb300318e909e550aeac0ab895afe8f">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/43/4by3/2021/03/08/43c94ccf47b541fb9cefcb86a5a136c8_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            CourtTV
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-ceb300318e909e550aeac0ab895afe8f-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-75d1e59af17883d14fe18ee0a6d8e2f2">
         <p>
          The news came after a huge crowd had gathered outside the Hennepin County Government Center ... holding signs that read “Hope,” "Reflect," “Stronger Together,” and “This is what community looks like." They had also gathered there Sunday.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-75d1e59af17883d14fe18ee0a6d8e2f2-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-72c38fef4c43d20ab6c88e64229d7f16">
         <p>
          There was also a huge law enforcement presence in the area to keep things under control ... though things look very much peaceful. Chauvin, who is out on a
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2020/10/07/george-floyd-cop-derek-chauvin-released-from-prison/">
           <strong>
            $1 million bond
           </strong>
          </a>
          , was seen inside the courtroom ... wearing a suit and face mask.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-72c38fef4c43d20ab6c88e64229d7f16-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-68692f4dfb02468d38e195d7af5cc616">
         <p>
          The ex-cop is charged with second-degree murder and manslaughter. He's accused of murdering Floyd after he was seen on video
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2020/05/26/minneapolis-police-department-brutality-african-american-man-dies-blocked-airway/">
           <strong>
            pressing his knee
           </strong>
          </a>
          on the back of Floyd's neck for
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2020/05/29/george-floyd-killing-news-conference-prosecutors-charges/">
           <strong>
            nearly 9 minutes
           </strong>
          </a>
          .
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-68692f4dfb02468d38e195d7af5cc616-->
       </div>

           <a class="btn social__btn social__btn--twitter js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"twitter-footer","pos":9}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:ed207b53-4b5e-4670-9980-0478b46cdb51" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/08/george-floyd-derek-chauvin-case-jury-selection-supporters-gather-courthouse/" onclick="window.open('https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F08%2Fgeorge-floyd-derek-chauvin-case-jury-selection-supporters-gather-courthouse%2F&amp;text=Derek%20Chauvin%20Jury%20Selection%20Delayed%2C%20Floyd%20Supporters%20Flock%20to%20Courthouse&amp;via=TMZ&amp;related=HarveyLevinTMZ', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">

      <article class="article" id="blogroll-2ad021c5-7124-43e4-ab00-2afe8aeb69dc">
       <div class="article__channel--viral">
       </div>
       <header class="article__header">
        <a class="article__header-link js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"headline","pos":10}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:2ad021c5-7124-43e4-ab00-2afe8aeb69dc" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/08/burger-king-women-belong-in-the-kitchen-scholarship-sexist/">
         <h2 class="article__header-title">
          <span class="article__hf1 text-uppercase h3">
           Burger King
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf2 text-uppercase h1">
           Women Belong in the kitchen ...
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf3 text-none h2">
           As Chefs, If They Want To!!!
          </span>
         </h2>
        </a>
        <h5 class="article__published-at">
         <ul class="social social--sm">
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Facebook" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--facebook js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"facebook-header","pos":10}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:2ad021c5-7124-43e4-ab00-2afe8aeb69dc" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/08/burger-king-women-belong-in-the-kitchen-scholarship-sexist/" onclick="window.open('http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F08%2Fburger-king-women-belong-in-the-kitchen-scholarship-sexist%2F', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">
            <span aria-label="Facebook" class="icon icon-facebook--white social__icon--facebook" role="img">
            </span>
            <span class="social__count">
             1.1K
            </span>
            <span class="sr-only">
             shares
            </span>
           </a>
          </li>
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Twitter" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--twitter js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"twitter-header","pos":10}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:2ad021c5-7124-43e4-ab00-2afe8aeb69dc" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/08/burger-king-women-belong-in-the-kitchen-scholarship-sexist/" onclick="window.open('https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F08%2Fburger-king-women-belong-in-the-kitchen-scholarship-sexist%2F&amp;text=Burger%20King%20Says%20Women%20Belong%20in%20the%20Kitchen%2C%20Sexist%20Culinary%20Campaign&amp;via=TMZ&amp;related=HarveyLevinTMZ', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">
            <span aria-label="Twitter" class="icon icon-sd icon-twitter--white" role="img">
            </span>
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <!--/.social-->
         3/8/2021 8:34 AM PT
        </h5>
        <!--/.article__posted-date-->
       </header>
       <div class="article__blocks">
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first" id="cb-d3954ad3de9354c7b910b833cebc06f6">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/17/4by3/2021/03/08/178e9de7187c4978b789f1bdc207e44f_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Getty
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-d3954ad3de9354c7b910b833cebc06f6-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-b5c3be814f16019087d3b4c533605e50">
         <p>
          Burger King has a funny way of promoting gender equality -- because it said something totally sexist about women ... as a way to plug a new initiative supporting them.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-b5c3be814f16019087d3b4c533605e50-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-6b461d6eac746640fdf7ccdff2f2a57a">
         <p>
          Yes, this is what honchos at BK's British office thought would be a good campaign to hype a new scholarship program -- tweeting early Monday, "Women belong in the kitchen."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-6b461d6eac746640fdf7ccdff2f2a57a-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-4c00a9ae17aec7abcbd702e08f692c7f">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/3f/4by3/2021/03/08/3febc0777d4743d691ba1886b194b92b_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-4c00a9ae17aec7abcbd702e08f692c7f-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-640b5f4a231864834440e74e8de72cd0">
         <p>
          As the Internet started dragging them, BK added ... "If they want to, of course. Yet only 20% of chefs are women. We're on a mission to change the gender ratio in the restaurant industry by empowering female employees with the opportunity to pursue a culinary career. #IWD."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-640b5f4a231864834440e74e8de72cd0-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-f49921dea887646a6ded7d177ffe2a81">
         <p>
          See what they did there? Piss off everyone with one disgustingly misogynistic tweet, then hit 'em with ... wait, we're doing a good thing!
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-f49921dea887646a6ded7d177ffe2a81-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-8788e85a93fddc4a2c78dcfa37c412dc">
         <p>
          BK says the scholarship is meant to uplift their female employees, who wanna move past fry cook and be bona fide chefs.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-8788e85a93fddc4a2c78dcfa37c412dc-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-4c750ea06c57ca448c41fd640c602352">
         <p>
          BTW ... March 8 is International Women's Day -- a worldwide holiday aimed at celebrating ladies everywhere. For some reason, Burger King ran with this as their #IWD campaign.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-4c750ea06c57ca448c41fd640c602352-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-5027b1775bc58faae905491c85ee798b">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/67/4by3/2021/03/08/6782082f1fd0423792f52704ef08c85a_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-5027b1775bc58faae905491c85ee798b-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-b93d34b6f552f4d8a86d38222e6dd8e8">
         <p>
          A couple hours after the in-poor-taste rollout ... Burger King UK added one last clarifying tweet -- "We are proud to be launching a new scholarship programme which will help female Burger King employees pursue their culinary dreams!"
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-b93d34b6f552f4d8a86d38222e6dd8e8-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-710d4a26c48c867f0a6ca9c0a4864263">
         <p>
          Talk about burying the lede, BK.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-710d4a26c48c867f0a6ca9c0a4864263-->
       </div>

           <a aria-label="Share on Twitter" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--twitter js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"twitter-header","pos":11}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:47ca1117-a8f0-43d2-909b-b4d4673748fe" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/08/racism-royal-family-evident-meghan-markle-broach-colonialism/" onclick="window.open('https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F08%2Fracism-royal-family-evident-meghan-markle-broach-colonialism%2F&amp;text=Racism%20in%20Royal%20Family%20Seemed%20Evident%20Early%20On%20in%20Meghan%27s%20Tenure&amp;via=TMZ&amp;related=HarveyLevinTMZ', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">
            <span aria-label="Twitter" class="icon icon-sd icon-twitter--white" role="img">
            </span>
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <!--/.social-->
         3/8/2021 8:09 AM PT
        </h5>
        <!--/.article__posted-date-->
       </header>
       <div class="article__blocks">
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first" id="cb-24ffcef235dd84a45242d1ad76475dac">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/85/4by3/2021/03/08/85a44166308a41488a39ba36ddbf5c81_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Getty
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-24ffcef235dd84a45242d1ad76475dac-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-8127e83d5767e4d366ab6f8c4420e7d9">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/meghan-markle/">
           <strong>
            Meghan Markle
           </strong>
          </a>
          's claims of racism against the Royal Family appear to be partially backed up by the fact this very issue came up early on -- remember the brooch?
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-8127e83d5767e4d366ab6f8c4420e7d9-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-e93eb37717116cc9098c825083b42aaa">
         <p>
          If ya don't,
          <strong>
           Princess Michael
          </strong>
          -- who's married to one of
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/queen-elizabeth-ii/">
           <strong>
            Queen Elizabeth
           </strong>
          </a>
          's cousins -- apologized back in late 2017 when she was called out for wearing a Blackamoor brooch to a Royal gathering Meghan attended ... the first Christmas lunch since getting with Harry.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-e93eb37717116cc9098c825083b42aaa-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-eba45d7e75b1e2e2915ad2c337741577">
         <p>
          The brooch depicts a dark-skinned person wearing a turban, and it's thought to glorify colonialism and servitude ... as that line of jewelry often portrays POC in lesser-than positions.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-eba45d7e75b1e2e2915ad2c337741577-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-b6b8dbdec20ea80645fa4ccc5cbb1ff5">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/91/4by3/2021/03/08/914993807f8840398a7f3444981753d9_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Getty
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-b6b8dbdec20ea80645fa4ccc5cbb1ff5-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-ddcd76ed9df8f047190a1bfd3941fd32">
         <p>
          Princess Michael said she meant nothing by it when she
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2017/12/22/meghan-markle-insult-queens-lunch-with-racially-insensitive-jewelry/">
           <strong>
            wore it to the lunch
           </strong>
          </a>
          , and wasn't trying to offend or send a message to Meghan specifically.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-ddcd76ed9df8f047190a1bfd3941fd32-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-dc6273685caff630fba206d9b0629da8">
         <p>
          Still, it's not a good look in light of what Meghan and
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/prince-harry/">
           <strong>
            Harry
           </strong>
          </a>
          alleged in the
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/07/meghan-markle-accuses-royal-family-racism-archie-dark-skin/">
           <strong>
            explosive tell-all
           </strong>
          </a>
          with
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/oprah-winfrey/">
           <strong>
            Oprah
           </strong>
          </a>
          -- namely, that they'd been informed by a member or members of the Royal Family that Archie's skin color could potentially be a problem, if he was born "too dark."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-dc6273685caff630fba206d9b0629da8-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-video-block canvas-video-block-blogroll canvas-video-block--default" id="cb-fd2e5ead835695193d980c7c39ddcff1">
