          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-1802829979-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-1802829979-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-1802829979-footer');
            hideSpinner();
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-1802829979-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-1802829979-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-1802829979-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-1802829979-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-1802829979'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-1802829979-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046-1802829979-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-08-030821-meghan-markle-oprah-1051465/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:3533e519-f220-41e8-89ae-ff016b652046',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });
         </script>

         <p>
          They wouldn't name the alleged perpetrator(s), but Harry
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/08/harry-meghan-markle-royal-family-not-reached-out-queen-elizabeth-prince-philip-not-racist/">
           <strong>
            did rule out
           </strong>
          </a>
          2 names in a follow-up chat ... saying neither Queen Elizabeth nor
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/prince-philip/">
           <strong>
            Prince Philip
           </strong>
          </a>
          uttered such words.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-a9eed02f1e4a288711cf52d1971c68d5-->

         <p>
          The Royal Family, of course, is quite vast ... so it could be anyone who might've said this.
         </p>
        </section>

          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-760171970-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-760171970-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-760171970-footer');
            hideSpinner();
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-760171970-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-760171970-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-760171970-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-760171970-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-760171970'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-760171970-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-8f7f7e8b-29bc-493f-a104-bff8cbbcd3ce-760171970-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-08-030721-meghan-markle-archie-1051458/',

                  }

            host: 'https://www.youtube-nocookie.com',

            },

        e.target.cueVideoById('e4pqOrP8a6E', 0);
      }

        swipeDiv.innerText = "Breaking News";

        $target.html(document.getElementById('cb-562646c63aaae9eb93189aba5c66bddc-765029927-failed').innerHTML);
      }

      function styleIframe(e) {
        var iframe = e.target.getIframe();
        iframe.classList.add('embed-responsive');
        if (!iframe.getAttribute('width')) {
          iframe.setAttribute('width', targetWidth);
        }
        if (!iframe.getAttribute('height')) {
          iframe.setAttribute('height', targetWidth / (16 / 9));
        }
      }

              window.TMZ.utils.loadYouTubeJs()
          .then(function initYouTubeBlock() {
            initPlayer(function onReady(e) {
              styleIframe(e);
              cueVideo(e);
                                        });
          }).catch(fail);
          });
         </script>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-562646c63aaae9eb93189aba5c66bddc-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-767cb4259918091f08cd8b24d738e384">
         <p>
          Oprah grilled Harry for details, but he refused to share any about what exactly was said ... or who allegedly said it. Basically, he's taking that to the grave -- but he did say this ... it was clear from the get-go with Meghan that race was something that was on the Royal Family's mind, and that it was going to be difficult to navigate.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-767cb4259918091f08cd8b24d738e384-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-434fd8c8e76806ef68ab03612d4d1553">
         <p>
          He said things were brought up to him about Meghan, like suggestions that she carry on with her acting career, as the Family supposedly didn't have enough money to support her or offer security for her. He also said the question was asked ... what would their kids look like?
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-434fd8c8e76806ef68ab03612d4d1553-->

  var response = 'unknown';

    window.TMZ.utils.loadTwitterJs().then(function (twttr) {

      });
    }).catch(reject);

      return;

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first" id="cb-fc8e4c9b2b47725b96012d97dfa1c763">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/42/4by3/2021/03/08/4213da79e24345d094d216ff102f8bdd_md.jpg"/>

           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            givingpledge.org
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>

        <!--/#cb-fc8e4c9b2b47725b96012d97dfa1c763-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-e3fde6431dbdffb6ffb5c01d033a81c9">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/mackenzie-bezos/">
           <strong>
            MacKenzie Scott
           </strong>
          </a>
          has a new husband -- a teacher at her kids' school -- and while marrying the ex-Mrs.
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/jeff-bezos/">
           <strong>
            Jeff Bezos
           </strong>
          </a>
          means the guy's suddenly mega-wealthy ... he's already giving it all away.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-e3fde6431dbdffb6ffb5c01d033a81c9-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-fb997d01e93f101b2bdf515f1ddc644c">
         <p>
          MacKenzie and
          <strong>
           Dan Jewett
          </strong>
          went public with their marriage over the weekend. Dan teaches science at Seattle Lakeside school ... the elite private institution Jeff and MacKenzie's 4 kids have attended.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-fb997d01e93f101b2bdf515f1ddc644c-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-ef427a439acfe680f6908a92e06886eb">
         <p>
          Sounds like Dan and Jeff might have met at PTA meetings over the years -- Bezos released a statement, saying ... "Dan is such a great guy, and I am happy and excited for both of them."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-ef427a439acfe680f6908a92e06886eb-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-862247777fd3994238c15633161ed9b7">
         <p>
          It's unclear exactly when MacKenzie -- who's reportedly worth about $53 billion -- tied the knot, but on Saturday Dan posted a message on The Giving Pledge website and promised to give away his wealth ... just like his new wife.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-862247777fd3994238c15633161ed9b7-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-4ea021be900b80c64944df1afc075694">
         <p>
          Dan wrote about his own passion for giving, and added, "And now, in a stroke of happy coincidence, I am married to one of the most generous and kind people I know, and joining her in a commitment to pass on an enormous financial wealth to serve others."
         </p>
        </section>

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-33ccb6c12972258a2b72ed0de8b9e518">
         <p>
          For those keeping score, MacKenzie's now one step ahead of Bezos in the "moving on" department. Jeff's been with GF
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/lauren-sanchez/">
           <strong>
            Lauren Sanchez
           </strong>
          </a>
          since he and McKenzie split in
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2019/01/09/jeff-bezos-divorcing-wife-160-billion-divorce/">
           <strong>
            January 2019
           </strong>
          </a>
          , but no wedding bells for them. Not yet.
         </p>
        </section>

         <div class="image-block">

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-9345bba59daffeec65e679e043181dba">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/piers-morgan/">
           <strong>
            Piers Morgan
           </strong>
          </a>
          <strong>
          </strong>
          had an on-air shouting match with a Black woman during his morning TV show over her claims
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/queen-elizabeth-ii/">
           <strong>
            Queen Elizabeth
           </strong>
          </a>
          is racist toward
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/meghan-markle/">
           <strong>
            Meghan Markle
           </strong>
          </a>
          .
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-9345bba59daffeec65e679e043181dba-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-77c7e6934fa5f9b5f72ea7b85ed03b66">
         <p>
          <strong>
           Dr. Shola Mos-Shogbamimu
          </strong>
          was one of the panelists who joined Piers Monday on "Good Morning Britain" to discuss
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/oprah-winfrey/">
           <strong>
            Oprah
           </strong>
          </a>
          's interview with
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/prince-harry/">
           <strong>
            Prince Harry
           </strong>
          </a>
          and Meghan -- and she ripped into the Royal family, calling it an institution rooted in white supremacy and racism.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-77c7e6934fa5f9b5f72ea7b85ed03b66-->

         <p>

         </p>

         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/31/4by3/2021/03/08/31d9319759cc4edaa3a08b314ca2312b_md.jpg"/>

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-04324a90581eb98bd7e58421db432878">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/bethenny-frankel/">
           <strong>
            Bethenny Frankel
           </strong>
          </a>
          has done an about-face, expressing sympathy for
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/meghan-markle/">
           <strong>
            Meghan Markle
           </strong>
          </a>
          and apologizing for going after her hard before she saw the interview.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-04324a90581eb98bd7e58421db432878-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-805cb3bc27146c14082f5fe3bdf2fe5a">
         <p>
          Hours before
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/oprah-winfrey/">
           <strong>
            Oprah
           </strong>
          </a>
          's interview aired, Bethenny went on a tear, saying, "Cry me a river ... the plight of being a game show host, fairly unknown actress, to suffering in a palace with tiaras &amp; 7 figure weddings for TWO WHOLE YEARS to being a household name with @Oprah on speed dial, fetching 7 m for interviews ..."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-805cb3bc27146c14082f5fe3bdf2fe5a-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-a419207b4feb1615a2020659fbb4988e">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/91/4by3/2021/03/08/91454a9825784aa18bcdb34945032efe_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-a419207b4feb1615a2020659fbb4988e-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-84afbaed69b373a0fa8aff81b49d7c9b">
         <p>
          Well, after the interview, Bethenny's
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/07/bethenny-frankel-mocks-meghan-markle-plight-oprah-interview/">
           <strong>
            tune changed
           </strong>
          </a>
          . She said, "I watched M &amp; H sit down. Emotional distress &amp; racism must feel suffocating &amp; powerless. I'm a polarizing, unfiltered (often to a fault) flawed person w a voice. When I hear of the interview during a pandemic, it felt like a surprising choice. I'm sorry if it hurt or offended you."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-84afbaed69b373a0fa8aff81b49d7c9b-->

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-e44cd50f-35f5-464b-bb4f-97c1508c982d-2052465550-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-e44cd50f-35f5-464b-bb4f-97c1508c982d-2052465550-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-e44cd50f-35f5-464b-bb4f-97c1508c982d-2052465550-footer');
            hideSpinner();
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-e44cd50f-35f5-464b-bb4f-97c1508c982d-2052465550-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-e44cd50f-35f5-464b-bb4f-97c1508c982d-2052465550-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-e44cd50f-35f5-464b-bb4f-97c1508c982d-2052465550-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-e44cd50f-35f5-464b-bb4f-97c1508c982d-2052465550-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-e44cd50f-35f5-464b-bb4f-97c1508c982d-2052465550'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-e44cd50f-35f5-464b-bb4f-97c1508c982d-2052465550-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-e44cd50f-35f5-464b-bb4f-97c1508c982d-2052465550-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-08-030721-meghan-markle-suicidal-thoughts-1051461/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:e44cd50f-35f5-464b-bb4f-97c1508c982d',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });
         </script>

           Megyn Kelly
          </strong>
          , however, was unmoved by the interview, saying, "Meghan Markle had no idea the Queen was different than a Hollywood celebrity? And she never googled Harry? Ummm..."

      <article class="article" id="blogroll-7138edc6-c78a-457d-84a0-8acc23ba45ed">
       <div class="article__channel--relationships">
       </div>
       <header class="article__header">
        <a class="article__header-link js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"headline","pos":16}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:7138edc6-c78a-457d-84a0-8acc23ba45ed" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/08/dustin-diamond-never-legally-married-despite-saying-jennifer-misner-wife-wedding-ring/">
         <h2 class="article__header-title">
          <span class="article__hf1 text-uppercase h3">
           Dustin Diamond
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf2 text-uppercase h1">
           Never Legally Married ...
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf3 text-none h2">
           Despite Saying He Was
          </span>
         </h2>
        </a>
        <h5 class="article__published-at">
         <ul class="social social--sm">
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Facebook" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--facebook js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"facebook-header","pos":16}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:7138edc6-c78a-457d-84a0-8acc23ba45ed" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/08/dustin-diamond-never-legally-married-despite-saying-jennifer-misner-wife-wedding-ring/" onclick="window.open('http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F08%2Fdustin-diamond-never-legally-married-despite-saying-jennifer-misner-wife-wedding-ring%2F', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">
            <span aria-label="Facebook" class="icon icon-facebook--white social__icon--facebook" role="img">
            </span>
            <span class="social__count">
             694
            </span>
            <span class="sr-only">
             shares
            </span>
           </a>
          </li>
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Twitter" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--twitter js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"twitter-header","pos":16}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:7138edc6-c78a-457d-84a0-8acc23ba45ed" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/08/dustin-diamond-never-legally-married-despite-saying-jennifer-misner-wife-wedding-ring/" onclick="window.open('https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F08%2Fdustin-diamond-never-legally-married-despite-saying-jennifer-misner-wife-wedding-ring%2F&amp;text=Dustin%20Diamond%20Was%20Never%20Legally%20Married%2C%20Despite%20Saying%20He%20Was&amp;via=TMZ&amp;related=HarveyLevinTMZ', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">
            <span aria-label="Twitter" class="icon icon-sd icon-twitter--white" role="img">
            </span>

          </li>
         </ul>
         <!--/.social-->
         3/8/2021 12:50 AM PT
        </h5>
        <!--/.article__posted-date-->
       </header>
       <div class="article__blocks">
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first" id="cb-b2ca216252adf664d1b4da582fa1a075">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/78/4by3/2021/03/05/78ce37d9f6c54f028ec521c509a7b6eb_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="media-swipe image-block__media-swipe">
           Exclusive
          </div>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Getty
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-b2ca216252adf664d1b4da582fa1a075-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-f8204b97a4122ec535e502b7e90bdaf7">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/dustin-diamond/">
           <strong>
            Dustin Diamond
           </strong>
          </a>
          was never married to
          <strong>
           Jennifer Misner
          </strong>
          -- despite publicly claiming they were husband and wife -- and their secret's only being revealed because of Dustin's death.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-f8204b97a4122ec535e502b7e90bdaf7-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-d9a9733e732a865fc13d7771c74bb1b2">
         <p>
          TMZ obtained the late 'Saved By The Bell' star's
          <a href="https://dam.tmz.com/document/ec/o/2021/03/05/ec4651a5d77d4f0480c2c42e275c4772.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" title="https://dam.tmz.com/document/ec/o/2021/03/05/ec4651a5d77d4f0480c2c42e275c4772.pdf">
           <strong>
            death certificate
           </strong>
          </a>
          , and under marital status it says "never-married." Of course, fans thought Dustin and Jennifer tied the knot back in the early 2000s ... and he'd even worn a wedding band.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-d9a9733e732a865fc13d7771c74bb1b2-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-document-block canvas-document-block-blogroll canvas-document-block--default" id="cb-1d3bab0f65c3d003adf99d732cc214df">
         <div class="document-block flex-column">
          <a class="media-link document-block__link js-track-link" data-container-ref="tmz:article:7138edc6-c78a-457d-84a0-8acc23ba45ed" data-node-ref="tmz:document-asset:document_pdf_20210305_ec4651a5d77d4f0480c2c42e275c4772" href="https://dam.tmz.com/document/ec/o/2021/03/05/ec4651a5d77d4f0480c2c42e275c4772.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
           <img class="img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/d9/4by3/2021/03/05/d91051f3cdad418da136a16fd80c3261_md.jpg"/>
           <div class="media-icon--overlay document-block__media-icon--overlay">
            <svg aria-hidden="true" height="64" role="img" viewbox="0 0 24 24" width="64" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
             <title>
              Document
             </title>
             <path d="M12 22A10 10 0 0 1 2 12 10 10 0 0 1 12 2v.7a9.3 9.3 0 1 0 0 18.6 9.3 9.3 0 0 0 0-18.6V2a10 10 0 0 1 10 10 10 10 0 0 1-10 10zm4-13v8H8V7h6l2 2zm-3-1v2h2l-2-2zm2 3h-3V8H9v8h6v-5z" fill="#fff">
             </path>
            </svg>
            <span class="media-icon-label document-block__media-icon-label">
             Launch Doc
            </span>
           </div>
           <footer class="media-footer document-block__media-footer">
            <span class="media-launch-text document-block__media-launch-text">
             read the death certificate
            </span>
            <span class="media-cta document-block__media-cta">
             Launch Doc
             <span class="media-footer-icon document-block__icon">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" height="24" role="img" viewbox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
               <title>
                Document
               </title>
               <path d="M12 22A10 10 0 0 1 2 12 10 10 0 0 1 12 2v.7a9.3 9.3 0 1 0 0 18.6 9.3 9.3 0 0 0 0-18.6V2a10 10 0 0 1 10 10 10 10 0 0 1-10 10zm4-13v8H8V7h6l2 2zm-3-1v2h2l-2-2zm2 3h-3V8H9v8h6v-5z" fill="#fff">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </span>
            </span>
           </footer>
          </a>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-1d3bab0f65c3d003adf99d732cc214df-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-f6d77110bd6029b89c90608a5f55b93c">
         <p>
          The real deal, according to Dustin's close friend,
          <strong>
           Dan Block
          </strong>
          is ... DD never legally married Jennifer. Dan tells TMZ, Jennifer was his girlfriend and he wore the ring as a way of showing his dedication to her when he traveled for work.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-f6d77110bd6029b89c90608a5f55b93c-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-5b3c885401c8a8d28a22819f87ba54be">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/88/4by3/2021/03/05/88b20b7cda2c4a04a5c5529a06a066a0_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-5b3c885401c8a8d28a22819f87ba54be-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-f94ab4410434bf750a0dd9642263166e">
         <p>
          Dustin went on
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/howard-stern/">
           <strong>
            Howard Stern
           </strong>
          </a>
          's show way back in 2006 trying to raise money to get his house out of his foreclosure after losing a child with Jennifer. At the time, he talked about marrying her -- but we're told he did that to get more sympathy while dealing with his dire financial crisis.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-f94ab4410434bf750a0dd9642263166e-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default" id="cb-033c1e4fc4ff96eba7dccb997e36c3eb">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/cc/4by3/2021/03/05/cca259486b244a10b5b9b5af921d83b4_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-033c1e4fc4ff96eba7dccb997e36c3eb-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-6bd447fe90e0c117a20baa13377ba5d7">
         <p>
          Dan says, in recent years, Dustin had wanted to clear up his marital status, and was particularly frustrated with his Wikipedia page -- which says he and Jennifer married in 2009 and separated in 2013.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-6bd447fe90e0c117a20baa13377ba5d7-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last" data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-3ae0cc7c0e50a9b602646dec4d8053bb">
         <p>
          TMZ broke the story ... Dustin
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/02/01/dustin-diamond-saved-by-the-bell-star-dead-44-stage-4-cancer-screech/">
           <strong>
            died last month
           </strong>
          </a>
          after a battle with Stage 4 lung cancer. His most recent girlfriend, Tash, was by his side when he passed away, and she now has
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/02/04/dustin-diamond-cremation-cremated-ashes-dad-girlfriend-saved-by-the-bell-screech/">
           <strong>
            some of his ashes
           </strong>
          </a>
          .
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-3ae0cc7c0e50a9b602646dec4d8053bb-->

Philip","bio":"Prince Phillip was born on 10 June 1921 as a Prince of Greece and Denmark. His family was deposed and he lived in France and finally went to boarding school in Gordonstoun in Scotland. Eventually he sent his boys there. When he was 18 he met 13 year old Princess (later Queen) Elizabeth, his third cousin from their descent from Queen Victoria, his second cousin once removed from their descent from King Christian IX of Denmark and fourth cousin once removed from their descent from King George III. They fell in love, but her father King George VI did not want them to get married right away. Before they became engaged he renounced his hereditary royal title and adopted the surname of his uncle Louis Mountbatten. They were engaged in 1947 and married on November 20th of that year. Before they married he was created His Royal Highness the Duke of Edinburgh, but was not given the title of Prince until 1957.\n\nAlmost a year after their wedding they had their first child, a boy, Charles Phillip Arthur George. In 1950 they had a daughter, Anne. They were followed by Andrew and Edward. After the death of his father in law in 1952 his wife became Queen Elizabeth II and he had to give up the Navy to help her being that he was now a royal consort. He has been active with services and takes on a lot of public engagements for his wife.\n\nIn the late 1970s he became a grandfather when his daughter Anne had two children, a boy called Peter and a girl named Zara. His eldest son Charles had a son William in 1982 and second son Henry in 1984. His second son Andrew had a daughter Beatrice in 1989 and second daughter Eugenie in 1991. Her sister Princess Margaret was born 4 years later. In 1936, when she was 10, her uncle, King Edward VIII (aka Duke of Windsor), caused a stir by abdicating the throne to marry a twice-divorced American named Wallis Warfield Simpson. His brother Albert was next in line to the throne, and he became George VI in honor of his father. She therefore became the Heiress Presumptive, meaning she would become Queen only if her parents did not have a son -- who would be king before her. At the age of 13, she met 18-year-old Prince Philip, her distant cousin. As her grandmother Queen Mary put it with more detail, they were third cousins through their descent from Queen Victoria (they are both great-great grandchildren of hers) second cousins once removed through their descent from King Christian IX of Denmark (her great-grandmother was Christian's daughter, his father was a descendant of his) and fourth cousins through their descent from George III (both of them being descendants of Queen Victoria -- she was his granddaughter). They fell in love and wanted to get married, but her father wanted to make sure it was real and not just because this was the first person she loved. Before they got married, he renounced his royal title as a Prince of Greece and Denmark, became a British subject, and adopted the surname of his uncle Louis Mountbatten. He was named Duke of Edinburgh shortly before they got married but was not made a Prince of the United Kingdom until 1957. They got married on November 20, 1947. One year later, they had a son, Charles Philip Arthur George. In 1950, they had Anne Elizabeth Alice; in 1960, Prince Andrew; and in 1964, Prince Edward.\n\nWhen they were in Kenya in 1952, they found out that her father had died of lung cancer so they returned as Queen and Consort. It was a busy time and got even busier. They worked at public engagements and, starting in the late 1970s, became grandparents. Anne had a son name Peter in 1977 and then a daughter named Zara in 1981 with her husband Captain Mark Phillips. Charles had William in 1982 and Henry in 1984 with his wife Diana. Andrew had Beatrice in 1988 and Eugenie in 1990 with his wife Sarah Ferguson.    <script>
    wbq.push(function manageSearchScreen() {
  var $search = $('.js__search-screen');
  var $searchCloseBtn = $('#search-screen-close-btn');
  var $searchToggleBtn = $('.js__btn--search-toggle');
  var $mastheadSearchOpenBtn = $('#masthead-search-open-btn');
  var $nav = $('.js__nav');

  function lockSearchFocus() {
    $searchCloseBtn.focus();
    document.addEventListener('focusin', focusSearchCloseBtn);
  }

  function focusSearchCloseBtn(event) {
    if (!$.contains(document.getElementById('search-screen'), event.target)) {
      $searchCloseBtn.focus();
    }
  }

  function unlockSearchFocus() {
    document.removeEventListener('focusin', focusSearchCloseBtn);
    $mastheadSearchOpenBtn.focus();
  }

  // close X used to dismiss mobile search overlay
  $searchToggleBtn.click(function (event) {
    // Toggle search screen visibility
    $search.toggleClass('search-screen--is-open');

    if ($search.hasClass('search-screen--is-open')) {
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        lockSearchFocus();
      }
      window.TMZ.utils.setAccessibilityFocusTrap('search-screen');
      $search.css('visibility', 'visible');
      setTimeout(function() {
        $nav.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    } else {
      window.TMZ.utils.removeAccessibilityFocusTrap();
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        unlockSearchFocus();
        $mastheadSearchOpenBtn.focus();
      }
      setTimeout(function() {
        $search.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    }

    // Hide nav
    if ($nav.hasClass('nav--is-open')) {
      setTimeout(function () {
        $nav.removeClass('nav--is-open');
      }, 300);
    }
    event.preventDefault();
  });
});
   </script>

  <script>
   wbq.push(function renderSubscribeToNewsletterModal() {
    function renderThankYou() {
      document.getElementById('newsletter-subscription-form').innerHTML = document.getElementById('newsletter-subscription-success').innerHTML;
      window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.destroyComponent('newsletter-subscription-lightbox-root', true));
    }

    function renderComponent(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      var lightboxDiv = document.createElement('div');
      var lightboxDivId = 'newsletter-subscription-lightbox-root';
      lightboxDiv.setAttribute('id', lightboxDivId);
      document.getElementById('lightbox-root').prepend(lightboxDiv);
      if (window.TMZ.utils.isValidEmail($('#newsletter-subscription-email').val())) {
        window.TMZ.renderComponent(
          'newsletter-subscription-lightbox-root',
          'newsletter-subscription-lightbox',
          {
            email: $('#newsletter-subscription-email').val(),
            id: 'newsletter-subscription-lightbox-root',
          },
        );
        document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.SUBSCRIBE_TO_NEWSLETTER_ACCEPTED, renderThankYou);
      } else {
        alert('Please enter a valid email.');
      }
    }

    $('#newsletter-subscription-form').on('submit', renderComponent);
  });
  </script>
